27/10/2024, 10:19โฏpm - +60 18-791 8584: FKE- ONLINE CLASS ON 29 OCT- 30 OCT 2024 IN CONJUNCTION WITH DEEPAVALI CELEBRATION

Dear undergraduate students.

The Ministry of Higher Education has released a media announcement that all teaching and learning from 28 October 2024 to 3 November 2024 will be conducted online or hybrid. 

In line with the directive by the Deputy Vice Chancellor (Academic and International) office dated 24 October 2024, the FKE Management has decided that classes on 28 October 2024 and 3 November 2024 will be conducted hybrid, where classes and laboratory sessions will be conducted physically face-to-face. 

Students celebrating Deepavali can join classes on these dates online (synchronous or asynchronous). 

29 and 30 October 2024 - online. 
28 October 2024 and 3 November 2024 - hybrid


Thank you, 

On behalf,
Deputy Registrar
Faculty of Electrical Engineering
